totalRows : rowsPerPage; const from = totalRows === 0 ? 0 : (currentPage - 1) * perPage + 1; const to = Math.min(currentPage * perPage, totalRows); $('#pagination-info').text('Showing ' + from + '–' + to + ' of ' + totalRows); } function renderControls(totalPages) { const $ctrl = $('#pagination-controls'); $ctrl.empty(); if (totalPages <= 1) return; const prevDis = currentPage === 1 ? 'btn-primary' : 'btn-default'; $ctrl.append('<button class=\"btn ' + cls + ' btn-xs pg-btn\" data-page=\"' + p + '\">' + p + '</button>'); } if (endP < totalPages - 1) $ctrl.append('<span style=\"padding:2px 6px;font-size:12px;\">…</span>'); if (endP < totalPages) $ctrl.append('<button class=\"btn btn-default btn-xs pg-btn\" data-page=\"' + totalPages + '\">' + totalPages + '</button>'); const nextDis = currentPage === totalPages ?
